## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="98241-1091">Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98241-1091">Windows Server 2008 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="98241-1092">Atributos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="98241-1092">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2008-r2-attributes)
